Guerrilla Forces Besiege Japanese Troops Near Erdaogouzi 30

(Harbin) The Japanese Iwasaki unit was besieged by more than 300 guerrillas near Erdaogouzi in northern Manchuria yesterday morning. As a result, five Japanese soldiers were seriously injured, and the guerrillas suffered no casualties. (Dispatch from the Chinese United News Agency on the 19th)

New Japanese Invention: All-Metal Car Wheels 31

Lightweight, Durable, and Without the Danger of Rupture; Can Be Used in Airplanes and Tanks

(Tokyo) The automobile manufacturing industry is one of the major sectors of the Japanese military industry today. In view of this fact, Mr. Iwamoto Dousei, the owner of the Iwamoto Industrial Works, recently invented a metallic car wheel. Because automobile wheels and tires are all foreign-made, Iwamoto decided to invent an all-metal car wheel for fear that business would be difficult to continue in the event of an emergency, and he succeeded. Its features are strong durability, no danger of tire rupture, light weight, and low cost. It can be used not only as a wheel for ordinary cars but also as a wheel for airplanes and tanks for military purposes. It has been understood by the military authorities and supported by powerful people in the financial world, and large-scale manufacturing has begun. (Dispatch from the Allied News Agency on the 19th)

Japanese Navy Decides to Establish Liquid Fuel Factory 32

Mitsui Changes Business Strategy to Establish Company to Cater to the Military

(Tokyo) In order to solve the fuel problem, the Japanese Navy Department previously sent Lieutenant Commander Yokota and fuel factory engineers to actively research the naval-style coal liquefaction method. At present, it has been announced that it has been completed, and 10 million yen has been invested in the Huaiyan plant of the North Korean Coal Industry Corporation to carry out manufacturing. It is planned to create a factory with an annual output of 50,000 tons recently and an annual output of 150,000 tons in the future to engage in manufacturing. The first phase of the plan can be fully realized before June next year. (Dispatch from the Chinese United News Agency on the 19th)

(Tokyo) The Japanese Mitsui zaibatsu, in view of the lessons of the February 26th Incident, has decided to modify its past profit-oriented business policy and invest in national defense to cater to the military's wishes. It plans to start by establishing a liquid fuel company in Hokkaido, with a capital of 20 million yen. It will increase investment after the business develops. It is expected to start construction in one year, with an annual production of 30 million tons. (Dispatch from the Chinese United News Agency on the 19th)

Philippine Military Inspection Report 33

Ten Years of Training Required to Resist Powerful Enemies; MacArthur Appointed Philippine Army General

(Manila) General MacArthur, the head of the US Philippine Military Inspection Group, reported on the inspection of the Philippine military over the past six months, indirectly discussing Japan's Asian strategy. This report was submitted to Congress today by President Quezon of the Autonomous Government. It stated that if the Philippines is oppressed by a strong neighbor, the United States will be in great difficulty and may be involved in the vortex of war. The Philippine reserve soldiers still need ten years of training to resist powerful foreign enemies. Moreover, the Philippines is isolated at sea, and to prevent the invasion by enemy countries, a huge sum of money must be spent on constructing bases to accommodate 300,000 people on Luzon Island. When submitting the report, Quezon appointed MacArthur as a general and requested Congressional approval as compensation for MacArthur's training of the autonomous government's national defense forces. According to the military inspection bill passed by the US Congress, MacArthur can hold military positions in the Philippines concurrently. Quezon declared today that when submitting this report, I sincerely wish to express to the US government and its people the gratitude of the Filipinos for their dispatch of talented people to consolidate the position of the Philippines. (Dispatch from the Kuomintang on the 19th)

(Manila) Former US Army Chief of Staff Major General MacArthur, who is now serving as a military advisor to the Philippine government, was today appointed as a general in the Philippine Army by the Philippine President. MacArthur is 56 years old, has rich military experience, and has extraordinary organizational skills. He graduated from the US West Point Military Academy in 1903 and subsequently served in the US military in the Philippines. He then went to Japan for two years. From 1906 to 1907, he served as an aide to President Roosevelt. During the European War, he was the first to lead American troops to the battlefield. In 1930, he served as the US Army Chief of Staff, becoming the youngest general in the US Army. He completed his term in 1934 and remained in office at the request of President Roosevelt. In 1935, he was hired by the Philippine government as a military advisor, specializing in training the army of the new republic. (Reuter's dispatch on the 19th)

Sun and Russian Observations of Solar Eclipse - Complete Success 34

Clear Weather Enables Capture of Valuable Material; Hokkaido Japanese Academic Group Declares Success

(Tokyo) A group of Japanese scientists observing the total solar eclipse in Huma, Amur River, Northern Manchuria, has reportedly achieved complete success. Huma is a remote mining area approximately one hundred miles northwest of Heihe. The group consisted of a joint team from the Shanghai Society of Natural Sciences and the Xijing Observatory. The weather was clear during the eclipse, allowing for the capture of images of the solar corona and the observation of changes in Earth's magnetism. A British scientific team observing in Hokkaido had no success due to heavy clouds during the eclipse. A Tokyo University team observing in Koshimizu also failed to achieve their desired results due to cloud cover. However, within the three-hundred-mile zone of totality across Japan, conditions were excellent with no cloud cover elsewhere. The Tokyo Astronomical Group and a Japanese Central Meteorological Group reportedly obtained extremely satisfactory results. Aircraft also acquired valuable material. (Nineteenth Reuters)

(Tokyo) The day of the black sun has arrived. Scientists worldwide have mobilized to observe the mysteries of the universe in this short two-minute period. The solar eclipse was first observed in the Mediterranean and traveled eastward at a speed of one kilo per second, passing over Greece, Turkey, the Black Sea, and central Siberia. It entered Japan over the Russian border, making landfall in Wakkanai, the northernmost tip of Hokkaido, at 3:17 PM. Its black shadow passed over Nakatombetsu, Esashi, Omu, Mombetsu, Memambetsu, and Kamishari before finally entering the Pacific Ocean from Nemuro and disappearing at the southern tip of the South Seas. Observation teams from China, Britain, America, India, Australia, Czechoslovakia, and Poland have selected Hokkaido as the most suitable location for observing the solar eclipse and are preparing for observations in the area. (Nineteenth Allied)

(Tokyo) According to reports from the Abashiri Observatory in Hokkaido, the weather in Hokkaido on the 19th was clear. According to the observatory's observations, a low-pressure system was present in the Heilongjiang area on the morning of the 19th, moving towards the northern Kuril Islands in the Pacific. West winds blew in the afternoon, and the weather was clear. (Seventeenth Allied)

Sapporo The solar eclipse, long awaited by scientists worldwide, was best observed from the ground at Nakatombetsu, Esashi, Omu, Mombetsu, Memambetsu, Kamishari, and other locations in Hokkaido. Astronomers from Japan, Britain, America, China, India, Australia, Czechoslovakia, and Poland gathered in these areas, hoping to gain insights from the two minutes spent peering through telescopes. The instant of transition from blackness to light determined the success or failure of this international observation effort. At Memambetsu and Abashiri, the Japanese team led by Dr. Saotome achieved great success due to the clear skies. However, the foreign team based in Kamishari failed because of sudden cloud cover. Japan therefore achieved a triumph. Dr. Stratton and Dr. Allen embraced and appeared quite frustrated. The observation results from other locations are as follows: Esashi - clear, great success; Nakatombetsu - the observation team and the crowd shouted "Banzai!" in celebration of their success; Wakkanai - great success; Mombetsu - great success; Memambetsu - clear, great success; Kamishari - failure due to cloud cover; Koshimizu - partially obscured by thin clouds, hindering observations. (Nineteenth Allied Press)

Shanghai's Haze Allows Glimpse of Partial Eclipse 37

Central News Agency: The solar eclipse, which was visible as a partial eclipse in Shanghai from 1:04 PM to 3:20 PM yesterday, was obscured by gray clouds from morning until night, making it impossible to observe. However, the ambient light during that time seemed dimmer than usual on cloudy days.

New News Agency says: According to the Central Astronomical Research Institute's measurements, the times for the partial eclipse seen in the city yesterday were as follows: first contact at 12:57 PM, maximum eclipse at 2:11 PM, and end of eclipse at 5:17 PM, extremely accurate. However, the weather yesterday was unfavorable, with heavy clouds and dim lighting. The sun briefly appeared around 10:30 AM but then disappeared. The haze was very thick at noon, and the general public, hoping to witness the miracle of the solar eclipse, was disappointed. Therefore, during the initial contact, it was impossible to discern the position of the sun in the dense clouds. Fortunately, the clouds gradually dispersed at 2:35 PM, and the sun was faintly visible through the moving clouds. At that time, people wearing colored glasses and looking upwards could see that the northwestern part of the sun was missing a corner, accounting for slightly less than one-third of the total area. As time progressed, the missing part gradually decreased. Just as the full restoration was expected at 3:05 PM, a cloud suddenly obscured it, and it was no longer visible. When the clouds dispersed at 3:37 PM, the fully restored sun radiated its light once more, illuminating the earth.

French Cabinet Issues Emergency Decree - Dissolving Right-Wing Military Groups 38

Remains of Russian Literary Giant Gorky Cremated Today 39

The cremation is scheduled for 6:00 PM on June 20 in Red Square. Funeral expenses will be paid by the government, and a committee will be established to handle Gorky's literary works and letters. (Eighteenth TASS)

A Brief Biography of Gorky 40

(Moscow) Gorky was born in 1868 in Nizhny Novgorod to a furniture maker. He lost his parents at a young age and worked as a servant in his teens, then as an apprentice in a handicraft shop, and later as a baker's assistant. In 1886, Gorky sought education in Kazan but was hindered by poverty. He associated with revolutionaries in Kazan and was arrested for the first time in 1889 for revolutionary activities. In 1891, he walked across Russia to Tiflis, working in a railway factory for a year, where he interacted with workers. In 1891, Gorky's first three works were published in a Tiflis newspaper, and his literary reputation grew. Several Russian newspapers and magazines published his novels. Due to his participation in the revolutionary movement, Gorky was imprisoned several times. By the end of 1899, Gorky was increasingly admired. He first went to St. Petersburg. In 1902, Gorky was elected an honorary member of the Academy of Sciences, but the Tsarist government revoked his qualifications. In 1903, Gorky returned from exile and assisted the Bolshevik Party's financial organization. He was arrested and exiled again in 1905, residing in Capri, where he continued his new work. During this time, Gorky became friends with Lenin, corresponded with him regularly, and actively participated in the Bolshevik Party's work. In 1913, Gorky returned to Russia and continued his literary work. After 1918, he actively participated in the cultural construction of the Soviet Republic. In 1921, Gorky contracted tuberculosis, and Lenin asked him to go abroad for rest and recuperation, returning to the country only in 1928. During this period, in addition to creating new art, Gorky often published works in foreign newspapers, opposing the destruction of the Soviet Union by White Russians abroad. Upon his return to the Soviet Union in 1928, he became a great proletarian writer, and with his immense talent, he participated in socialist creative work. His literary and social activities were highly regarded, not only for his extensive dramatic work but also for his dedication to the working class and his brilliant writings devoted to the victory of communism, which earned him such admiration. In 1929, he was elected to the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union. In the following years, Gorky continued to dedicate himself to social and political work. He published numerous works, edited and founded several important magazines, and as chairman of the Soviet Writers' Union, greatly contributed to the development of Soviet literature and young writers. Gorky was a most great artist, practitioner, and enthusiastic revolutionary, who throughout his life, devoted his immense talent and expressed the highest voice of humanity, becoming the most perfect exemplar in the world. (TASS)

Preliminary Negotiations Underway on Straits Defense Issue 42

Turkish Demands Expected to be Accepted - Mediterranean Pact Also Under Discussion

(London) The signatory nations of the Treaty of Lausanne are scheduled to hold a conference on June 22 in Montreux, Switzerland, to discuss the re-militarization of the Dardanelles and Bosporus straits. The countries involved are currently engaged in preliminary diplomatic negotiations. It is reported that these nations are generally agreeable to Turkey's demands (i.e., re-militarizing the straits), but one crucial issue remains to be resolved: the maximum tonnage of warships permitted to pass through the straits. Regarding this, Britain believes that since Turkey will be able to establish defensive installations in the straits, it can closely monitor the passage of any warship, negating the need for a tonnage limit. Furthermore, once sanctions against Italy are lifted, Italy may attend the Montreux conference, making the formation of a Mediterranean pact possible. Therefore, the ongoing preliminary negotiations among the countries involved have also touched on the issue of the Mediterranean pact. (Eighteenth Havas)

Resolutions of the Legislative Yuan 50

Rent Disputes

No Need to Enact a Mediation Law

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan convened its 63rd meeting on the morning of the 19th, attended by 63 members including Lin Bin, etc. President Sun Ke and Secretary-General Liang Hancao were excused due to illness, with Secretary Chen Haicheng substituting. The matters discussed were as follows:

Further amendments to the Organizational Law of the Ministry of Finance were resolved and passed, adding a provision to Article 23 of the law stating that the Ministry of Finance may, when necessary, employ three to seven specialist members. Further amendments to the Organizational Law of the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance were resolved and passed. Article 12 of the law, which originally stipulated that the Chief Accountant of the Customs Administration was under the direction of the Director-General of the Customs Administration, was amended to be under the supervision and direction of both the Director-General of the Customs Administration and the Chief Accountant of the Ministry of Finance. Article 14 was amended to state that external official documents of the Customs Administration shall be issued in the name of the Ministry of Finance, but with regard to the following matters, orders may be issued by the Administration: 1. Matters that should be relayed and instructed in accordance with the Ministry's orders; 2. Matters that are supervised and carried out in accordance with the methods stipulated in the Ministry's orders; 3. Matters that have been submitted to the Ministry for approval. Further amendments to the Organizational Law of the Taxation Administration of the Ministry of Finance were resolved and passed, amending Articles 18 and 19 of the law according to the examples of Articles 12 and 14 of the Organizational Law of the Customs Administration in the second case. , Amendments to the Organizational Law of the Salt Administration of the Ministry of Finance were resolved and passed, amending Article 23 of the law according to the example of Article 14 of the Organizational Law of the Customs Administration in the second case. Article 24, which originally stipulated the establishment of a Chief Accountant, was amended to a Chief Accountant, subject to the supervision and direction of the Salt Administration and the Chief Accountant of the Ministry of Finance. The Legislative and Land Law Committees reported on the examination of the Draft Mediation Law for Rent Disputes, and it was resolved to pass it according to the examination report. There is currently no need to enact this law. The reasons are as follows: The reason for designating this case was to stipulate the standards for housing rents and rent increases and decreases, so that landlords and tenants have something to follow, and to establish a mediation committee to seek mediation of rent disputes, and to separately stipulate penalties to ensure the effectiveness of mediation. After review by the Yuan, the following conclusions were reached: Regarding the standard of housing rents, the standard of housing rents varies from place to place, and it is difficult to uniformly regulate it. The case was drafted by the Executive Yuan and submitted to the Ministry of Industry. At the time of drafting, the Land Law had not yet been implemented. Now that the Land Law has been implemented since March 1 of this year, if there is a situation as stipulated in Article 162 of the Land Law, the provincial and municipal governments can base the standard rent for houses on the provisions of the Land Law. The rent standard set in the case, the maximum limit, shall not exceed 12% of the annual interest of the combined land price and construction cost, which is difficult to implement according to the current situation in various places. This is one reason. Regarding the standards for rent reduction and rent increase, Article 442 of the Civil Law already has provisions for the increase or decrease of real estate rents. If there is a dispute, it can be directly resolved by the court. This is the second reason. Regarding the mediation agency and procedures for rent disputes, Articles 402 and 409 of the Civil Procedure Law both have clear provisions. The organizational laws of cities and counties also have their own regulations regarding civil mediation, which are sufficient to be followed, and the organization of the mediation committee stipulated in the case may not be able to resolve disputes, or even be counterproductive. This is the third reason. Regarding the provisions of fines, the case imposes penalties on those who fail to fulfill the mediation agreement or who file a lawsuit without mediation, which is inappropriate. This is the fourth reason. The above are the main points of the case. According to the results of the review, if all are deleted and revised, there seems to be no need to enact a separate law at present. The Finance and Legislative Affairs Committees reported on the review of the Draft Regulations on Savings for Civil Servants. It was resolved that the review report of the two committees should be passed, and the case should be temporarily deferred until the amendment of the Central Bank Law is passed, and the articles of association of the Central Trust Bureau are reviewed and passed together before reconsideration. The Finance Committee reported on the drafting of the Implementing Regulations for the Fiscal Revenue and Expenditure System Law. It was resolved to return it to the committee for review and seek the opinion of the Ministry of Finance. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 19th)

(Nanjing) Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, regarding the further amendment of the Organizational Law of the Ministry of Finance, previously submitted the original text of the proposal to the Executive Yuan, stating that the Organizational Law of the Ministry of Finance passed by the Legislative Yuan has inevitable difficulties in implementation based on the facts, and it is proposed to make appropriate amendments to facilitate implementation. The articles that should be amended are listed as follows: Article 14 of the Organizational Law of the Customs Administration, Article 19 of the Organizational Law of the Taxation Administration, and Article 23 of the Organizational Law of the Salt Administration all list certain matters to be carried out in the name of the Ministry of Finance. In addition to the listed items, they can be carried out in the name of the Administration or the Bureau. The Ministry of Finance is in charge of all financial administration, and all external affairs should be approved by the Ministry. If the above articles are followed, listing the Ministry's orders in the articles is actually equivalent to restricting the Ministry's orders, while the issuance of Administration or Bureau orders has no scope, which is difficult to integrate and supervise. It is proposed to change it to state that all external official documents should be issued in the name of the Ministry of Finance, but with regard to the following matters, orders may be issued by the Administration: Matters that should be relayed and instructed in accordance with the Ministry's orders, Matters that are supervised and carried out in accordance with the methods stipulated in the Ministry's orders, Matters that have been submitted to the Ministry for approval. 2. Article 24 of the Organizational Law of the Salt Administration, the Salt Administration shall establish one Chief Accountant, who is under the direction of the Director of the Salt Administration. According to the Accounting Law and the Provisional Regulations on the Handling of Annual Budget Accounting Statistics of Various Agencies by the Accounting Department of the National Government, the accounting of each Administration and Bureau should be subject to the supervision and direction of the personnel in charge of annual budget accounting statistics of the higher-level agency. The Salt Administration is subordinate to the Ministry of Finance, and its rank is equal to the accounting personnel of other directly subordinate agencies of the Ministry of Finance. It is proposed to change the establishment of a Chief Accountant to a Chief Accountant, who should be subject to the supervision and direction of the Chief Accountant of the Ministry of Finance. As for Article 12 of the Organizational Law of the Customs Administration and Article 18 of the Organizational Law of the Taxation Administration, the phrase "the Chief Accountant is under the direction of the Director" should also be amended to "subject to the supervision and direction of the Director and the Chief Accountant of the Ministry of Finance." 3. Article 27 of the current Organizational Law of the Ministry, which stipulates that the Ministry of Finance may employ consultants and specialist members as necessary for business, should be deleted. Financial matters are complex and varied, and it is necessary to employ specialized personnel to assist in research. It should still be supplemented. The above articles should be forwarded to the Central Political Council and submitted to the Legislative Yuan for amendment. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 19th)

(Nanjing) The Legislative and Financial Affairs Committees of the Legislative Yuan were previously ordered to review the draft provisions on the exercise of authority over the budget accounting section in the organizational laws of various agencies. After review, it is proposed to expressly stipulate the number of personnel and the exercise of authority for this item in the organizational laws of various central agencies. As for the number of personnel, it was originally proposed to determine it by referring to the proportion of personnel in each agency. However, according to the results of the investigation, the actual number of personnel currently used by various agencies has exceeded the number stipulated in the current law. If the number of budget accounting personnel is stipulated according to the current law, it may hinder the facts. If the current number of personnel is used as the standard, then the current number of personnel has no legal basis. It was specially submitted to the Yuan meeting on the 19th for instructions. President Sun instructed the two committees to first draft a method and submit it for approval. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 19th)

Solar Eclipse Conditions in Various Places 59

(Beiping) The 19th was the date of the total eclipse. Many citizens of Beiping looked up at the sky and paid attention to the observation. Unfortunately, the sky was dim and the sunlight was hazy, lacking clarity. From 12:30, about two-tenths of the eclipse was visible. At 1:20, four-tenths of the eclipse was clearly distinguishable. The eclipse ended at 3:14. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 19th)

(Nanjing) During the solar eclipse on the 19th, a partial eclipse was seen in the capital. The Central Observatory failed to observe the initial eclipse at around 12:50 due to cloud cover. The clouds cleared at 1:03 p.m., and the solar eclipse had already begun. Twelve photos were taken successively, which differed from the forecast by about one and a half seconds. At the same time, a large sunspot, five prominences, and five dark lines on the solar surface were observed on the spectroscope. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 19th)

(Lanzhou) The solar eclipse seen in Lanzhou on the 19th lasted from 12:45 p.m. to 1:00 p.m., with only one-tenth of the eclipse visible. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 19th)

(Nanjing) During the solar eclipse on the 19th, the Purple Mountain Observatory took twelve photos successively and measured the time of the end of the eclipse at 3:17:25.5, which differed from the forecast by about one and a half seconds. At the same time, a large sunspot, five prominences, and five dark lines on the solar surface were observed on the spectroscope. (Special dispatch on the 19th)

Mingguang: Today at noon, the solar eclipse had an obscurity of about one-eighth and recovered at 3:00 p.m. (Special dispatch on the 19th)

Fujian Province Establishes a Special Business Tax Consolidation Office 60

The entire province is divided into three special zones for unified management

(Fuzhou) The Department of Finance convened the directors of the special business tax bureaus of various jurisdictions to discuss the consolidation of business taxes and decided to establish a Special Business Tax Consolidation Office, with positions such as Director, Section Chief, and Secretary. The monthly budget is more than 5,000 yuan. It is scheduled to be established on July 1. The consolidation principles are divided into three types: A. Imported goods, B. Goods produced in the province, and C. Local products. The original system is changed and merged into the special tax bureaus to seek unified tax revenue. It is to completely include export goods such as tea, bamboo, wood, and paper, import goods such as coal oil, etc., and goods that are both exported and imported, such as sugar, which has foreign sugar and native sugar. The various special taxes of these three types are consolidated and unified. The entire province has a total of three special zones: Minhou, Xiamen, and Sandu. Each zone has one Director who is solely responsible for the unified management. A special tax office is established in the provincial capital to carry out the orders of the Department of Finance and supervise the special tax bureaus in the three zones to step up their work. After the consolidation of various business taxes is completed, the tax rates will be revoked. The tax rate for imported goods will be increased, and the tax rate for goods produced in the province will be reduced to seek fairness. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 19th)

Gold and Silver

London gold price, today is 138 shillings 6 pence, down 1 pence from yesterday.

British American: The London foreign exchange market was very quiet today, lacking excitement. The price of the pound was relatively weak. The opening price of the British-American exchange rate was five dollars and three cents, the same as the closing price of the US-British yesterday. It fell by two-five after one hour, and then rebounded 0625 at 1 pm, to five dollars and two cents 8125.

Securities

New York: The market opened this morning, and the market showed sluggishness and unevenness. Steel, utilities, and steel stocks all loosened due to profit-taking. Later, speculative pressure stretched, causing most securities to be affected. At 11 o'clock, the price of major securities rose from zero to one pound from yesterday's closing. However, near noon, popularity showed stability due to new buying, and most of the lost points recovered. The market price of New York securities is listed on the left.

Japan Expands Tianjin General Consulate 88

Establishing Consular Sub-Branches in Strategically Important Locations; Increasing Police Stations Along the Ping-Han and Jin-Pu Lines to Protect the Special Trade of Japanese and Korean Nationals

Tianjin Correspondence: The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs' expansion of the Tianjin General Consulate, the plan for which was previously discussed by the Director of the East Asian Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Mr. Kuwashima, who came to Tianjin for consultations, has been decided. After Kuwashima returned home, he passed through Shanghai and met with the newly appointed Ambassador Kawagoe, exchanged opinions, and then returned home to report. The Tianjin Japanese General Consulate has now begun preparations to expand the consulate. The reason is to protect the safety of overseas Chinese along the Jin-Pu and Ping-Han lines, the special trade of Japanese and Korean nationals, and the right to reside in various inland areas. It is said that since this spring, the number of Japanese and Korean overseas Chinese has increased, and they are scattered throughout the Ping-Han and Jin-Pu lines. There is no residential safety, and conflicts occur with local officials from time to time. In the future, in order to avoid disputes, the Japanese consulate should directly handle the matter, establish consular sub-branches in key locations, and police stations. The Tianjin Japanese Police Department will increase its patrol officers by more than 80 and dispatch them to various locations for service. Regarding the location of establishment, General Consul Tajiri dispatched Police Inspector Fujii, the head of the Security Section of the Police Department, and Officer Uetsuma to Cangxian, Jinghai, Botouzhen, and Dongguang on the Jin-Pu Line on the 15th of this month to investigate. The scheduled itinerary is eight days, and they will return to Tianjin on the 23rd to report. After the report, they will go to Changxindian, Shijiazhuang, Baoding, Xingtai, and other places on the Ping-Han Line to investigate. The proposed sites for consular sub-branches are Cangxian, Baoding, and Shijiazhuang. Police stations will be set up in other locations. In addition, for matters that are not within the jurisdiction of the Tianjin General Consulate but have close connections, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has decided to establish a Taiyuan consulate, sending one consul and one vice-consul, and four or five staff members to handle all affairs of overseas Chinese. It will be realized at the same time as the consular sub-branches along the Ping-Han and Jin-Pu lines.

The four ministries of Japan, including the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, have reached many resolutions on the development of cotton production and the collection of wool textiles in North China. The Ministry of Colonial Affairs is the center for researching programs and adopting the method of division of labor and cooperation. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs is responsible for negotiating with our Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Finance is responsible for negotiating tariff agreements, and the Ministry of Commerce and Industry is responsible for industrial design. In order to realize the plan as soon as possible, the four ministries specially organized a North China Affairs Investigation Team, led by the Section Chief of the Cultivation Department of the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, comprising more than 30 people. They departed from Tokyo on June 3, arrived in Northeast China first, and arrived in Tianjin early on the 12th. Immediately, the Tianjin Japanese General Consulate sent staff to introduce them to relevant parties for investigation. The cotton and sheep investigation team, led by team leader Funabashi, with a total of nine members, went to Ping on the 15th and transferred to Inner Mongolia and Chahar to conduct inspections. The cotton production investigation team worked in Tianjin for a week, went to Ping on the 22nd, and transferred to Baoding on the 25th, and went to Dingxian, Zhengding, and Shunde to investigate separately. On the 30th, they will go to Zhengzhou and Chuzhou in Henan, then transfer to Haizhou, go to Qingdao on July 5, go to Jinan on the 11th, go to Shanghai on the 14th, and return home on the 17th. After the four ministries wait for the team to return home and report, they will formulate a plan and promote it through diplomatic means, and realize it within this year. (17th)

Zhang Zizhong Takes Office as Mayor of Tianjin 89

Qin Dechun Represents Song Zheyuan in Three Points

Tianjin Correspondence: The change of mayor in Tianjin, which had been brewing for a couple of weeks, was only decided a few days ago. The authorities were afraid of complications in diplomacy, so they temporarily concealed the truth and promoted a confusing propaganda. It was not until the 16th that the stalemate was broken, and the Hebei-Chahar Political Council ordered Xiao Zhenying to resign, transferred Zhang Zizhong to the post of Chairman of Chahar Province, and sent Liu Ruming, the commander of the 41st Division of the 29th Army, to succeed him. The personnel handover procedures have been completed for the first stage. In terms of political and governmental procedures, on the one hand, Zhang and Liu were instructed to take over the matter first, and on the other hand, they were telegraphed to the Executive Yuan to request the Central Standing Committee to recognize and formally issue an order, but they were still unwilling to make it public to the outside world. On the morning of the 17th, the authorities ordered Zhang Zizhong to rush to Tianjin to take office that day. Because his 38th Division was transferred from Zhangjiakou to Ping, the military transport was not completed, so he took care of it in Ping, and it was not until 1:30 pm that he took a special train from Beining, accompanied by Ma Yanchong, the Secretary-General of the Chahar Provincial Government, and Zhang Kexia, the Chief of Staff of the 38th Division, to Tianjin. Song Zheyuan also arrived in Tianjin at 5 pm that day. It was originally scheduled to take over at 5 pm that day, but because it was too late to rush, the ceremony was held at 10 am on the 18th. That night, Song summoned Zhang and the heads of various bureaus in the city at his private residence, and made some clarifications on the personnel changes, and gave some instructions on diplomacy and politics, summarizing the opinions of the public. At 10 am on the 18th, leading figures from all walks of life came to the Municipal Government to attend the ceremony. The dignitaries who attended included Wang Yitang, Li Tingyu, Gao Lingwei, Lin Shize, Chen Juesheng, Liu Jialuan, and the heads of the Municipal Public Security, Social Affairs, Public Works, Finance, and Health Bureaus, Sun Weidong, Liu Donggan, Liu Yushu, Chang Hongjun, and Li Zaizhong, and four or five hundred representatives from all walks of life. After the ceremony was performed, Qin Dechun represented Song Zheyuan in his instructions, which roughly stated that Tianjin is an important commercial port in North China, with a vast area and a dense population, where Chinese and foreigners live together. There are many things that should be done to revitalize and reform. Mayor Zhang has been in the military for many years and has made outstanding achievements. In recent years, he has governed Chahar and has been praised for his political voice. Today, he comes to lead Tianjin, and he should be able to use his past achievements to set an example for politics, and he will surely have good harvests in the future. I only offer three points of hope: 1. The country is based on the people, and officials are set up for the people. The foundation of politics should be the welfare of the people. As the ancients said, like what the people like, and hate what the people hate. I hope that Mayor Zhang will act on the public opinion of all citizens and seek the interests of the citizens. 2. The soundness of the country requires good politics, and the good of politics requires integrity first. I hope that Mayor Zhang will continue his past spirit of integrity, supervise his subordinates, and move forward. 3. Tianjin is a place where Chinese and foreigners live together, and diplomacy is important. I hope that Mayor Zhang will adhere to the central government's principle of good neighborliness, the principle of mutual benefit, and strive for friendship and peace. In times of peace, treat each other with courtesy, and in times of trouble, argue with reason. I think the gentry of Tianjin will be able to love and help, and the future is bright, which can also be predicted.

Then Zhang Zizhong gave a speech, which roughly stated that today Zizhong takes office as the mayor of Tianjin, and it is a great honor to have guests from all walks of life attending the ceremony. Tianjin is an important commercial port in North China. Since Mayor Xiao resigned due to illness, the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee has been extremely concerned about local security. The position of mayor cannot be without someone responsible for it for a day. He specially ordered Zizhong to act as an agent temporarily. I know that I am not capable enough to shoulder the heavy responsibility, but as a soldier, I only know how to obey orders. In the future, in terms of politics, I will eliminate all bad habits and establish a style of integrity under the principle of benefiting the country and the people, not telling lies, and not harboring selfish intentions, and strive to achieve a state of political clarity. Regarding local security, I will do my best to maintain it. In addition, such as relieving the people's livelihood, prospering the market, and rectifying the city appearance, I will also do my best to work hard to seek welfare for the people. Regarding diplomatic matters, Tianjin is a place where Chinese and foreigners live together. Zizhong is determined to stand on the position of his own duties, uphold the intention of good neighborliness, and hope to make efforts for coexistence and co-prosperity in the spirit of mutual benefit and equality. The standard of employing people is that anyone who is loyal to his duties will never be changed. If he is not competent or does not fulfill his duties, he will naturally be unable to help, so that people can make the most of their talents. However, Zizhong has been in the army for a long time and is not familiar with politics. I still hope that people from all walks of life will give me advice at any time and correct my shortcomings. The ceremony ended at about 11 o'clock, and photos were taken in the courtyard and dispersed. Shi Jisheng, the Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, handled the handover on behalf of Xiao, and resigned and went to Ping in the afternoon of the same day. The vacancy was filled by Ma Yanchong, the Secretary-General of the Chahar Provincial Government who came with Zhang, and took office on the same day.

Zhang Zizhong, courtesy name Jinchen, is 46 years old, from Linqing County, Shandong Province. He graduated from a law and politics school. In the third year of the Republic of China, he joined the army. In the fifth year, he served as a platoon leader of the 16th Mixed Brigade of the Army. In the 68th year, he was promoted to the model company commander of the brigade. In the eighth year, he was promoted to camp adjutant. In the tenth year, he was promoted to battalion commander. In the thirteenth year, he was promoted to the head of the Student Corps of the Northwest National Army. In the fifteenth year, he served as the brigade commander of the 15th Brigade of the Army. In the sixteenth year, he was promoted to the principal of the Second Group Army Military Academy, and concurrently served as the commander of the 28th Division. In August of the seventeenth year, it was changed to the commander of the 25th Division of the Central Land Vehicle. In the eighteenth year, it was changed to the 6th Division of the National Army, and he still served as the commander. In January of the twentieth year, it was changed to the 38th Division of the 29th Army, and he still served as the commander. In October of the twenty-fourth year, he served as a member of the Chahar Government and Chairman of the Province. He is now transferred to the Mayor of Tianjin. (18th)

Second Theft in the Forbidden City; Large Number of Antiques Lost from Qianqing Palace 90

Internal Personnel Suspected; One Person Has Been Apprehended and is Under Interrogation; Beiping Correspondence: After the theft in the Palace Museum and the southward transportation of antiques, there are not many left in Beiping. However, there are still quite a few valuable ones. After verification in the 23rd year, they were sealed up separately. However, there have been rumors of theft in recent years. Inside the iron fence behind the throne in the Qianqing Palace is where the verified antiques are stored. On the 18th, Palace Museum staff went to collect antiques and discovered that the fence lock had been broken and the stored antiques were in disarray. The report was given to Yu Heyin, the head of the preservation section of the museum, and then to Zhang Tingji, the head of the general affairs office. The report was given to President Ma Heng, and team leader Dong Yinfu and others were sent to reinvestigate. It was discovered that the antiques in that place were the antiques that had been verified by the verification committee in the 23rd year. After clearing the register, Zhao Ziang's calligraphy of Ma's true work was lost, and he tried his best to take it away, leaving the shaft behind. In addition, twelve white jade Ruyis, two vegetable Ruyis, one coral Ruyi, celebrity calligraphy and paintings and forty-three imperial folding fans, seventeen enamel watches of various types, and one ancient bronze incense burner were also lost. The rest are still under reinvestigation. At 2:00 pm, Qian Zongchao, the inspector of the Public Security Bureau, Zhang Liangchen, the head of the detective squad, and Qing Yin, the head of the Sixth District Office, jointly investigated the truth with the staff of the Palace Museum. Ma Heng also sent Bai Guiliang, the captain of the guard team of the museum, to investigate, and believed that it was done by internal personnel. As a result, a suspect has been detected, and he was still being interrogated on the night of the 18th. (18th)

Japanese Ronin Increasingly Smuggling at Jinan Station 91

Assaulting and Humiliating Road Police and Anti-Smuggling Personnel

Jinan Correspondence: Smuggling in North China is becoming increasingly rampant, and there is still no effective way to stop it. In recent days, the number of smuggled goods transported from Tianjin to Jinan has been increasing. There is almost no passenger space on third-class carriages. The goods are mainly rayon, sugar, and cigarette paper, followed by Biji formal dress woolen cloths. All of them are handled by Korean ronin. These goods are loaded on the 305 train from Pingpu to Jinan, which arrives at 9:40 am every day. Not only do they not pay customs duties, but they also do not have railway transport permits. It is said that when loading the train in Pingjin, they are thrown from outside the window to the inside, regardless of whether there are passengers. Therefore, passengers in the car are often injured. After arriving in Jinan, they are still thrown out of the window, destroying all the car window glass. After unloading, they force porters to carry them outside the station and load them onto cars or handcarts that they have prepared. Although our country's anti-smuggling inspection office has been established and has detained smuggled goods several times, they have been forcibly taken away and police and anti-smuggling personnel have been repeatedly assaulted and humiliated. In recent days, the amount of smuggled goods has been even greater, and ronin are rampant on the train. This morning (17th), a martial drama occurred. Staff of the anti-smuggling office, road police from the police section, and two passengers were all assaulted and humiliated, which is outrageous. The course of events is recorded as follows: Today (17th), the 305 train from Pingpu to Jinan, which arrived at 9:47 am, was full of smuggled goods packed in sacks and straw bags on third-class carriages, including rayon, white sugar, and cloth, totaling 358 pieces. After the train arrived at the station, as usual, 60 to 70 ronin who escorted and picked up the train threw the goods out of the window onto the platform, and then handed them over to the porters to carry them outside the station. Today, while the unloading was taking place on the platform, two passengers, each carrying a small camera, were filming the smuggled goods. Their intention was only driven by curiosity. Unexpectedly, they were discovered by the smugglers, who rushed forward and smashed the cameras, and beat the photographers. At this time, the chief of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Police Section was at the station, and went forward to persuade them in order to maintain order. However, the ronin were unreasonable and behaved like mad dogs, and assaulted the road police, patrol chiefs, and patrol officers. The ronin were all carrying canes and shouting loudly. Those who were beaten had their noses broken and blood flowed out. There were other passengers on the station who were also beaten occasionally. In order to avoid causing trouble, the patrol chief of the section recalled the road police to the police section when surrounded. After assaulting people, the ronin were still angry, and some of them were still looking for people to beat inside the station. Even a small number went to the office of the anti-smuggling personnel in the stationmaster's office, dragged three anti-smuggling inspectors out and beat them in groups. Although people surrounded them to protect them, the three had been beaten. Li Tonghua, the deputy director of the anti-smuggling office, and Ye Yuchun, the director of Jinan, were spared from the disaster because they were wearing Western clothes and not anti-smuggling uniforms. When the conflict occurred, passengers, except for those who escaped from the station, those who watched the situation could not help but shed tears and lamented the misery of a weak country. After receiving a telegram from the station, the Jinan Japanese Consulate sent personnel to the station. At that time, the siege had been lifted. The ronin claimed to the Japanese Consulate that they had been beaten. Later, our country's police section and anti-smuggling office told them the reason and said that the photography was not very intentional, but the Japanese Consulate still did not believe it. At 11 o'clock, the personnel of the Japanese Consulate returned, and the storm temporarily ended.

Local News

Qujiang Wharf Groundbreaking Ceremony Today 108

President Kong Personally Presides Over the Ceremony The First Phase of Construction to Be Completed by Year-End

The Central Bank's investment in the construction of the Qujiang Wharf has been underway for over a year. The first phase of the project is scheduled for completion by the end of this year, and the various buildings are already taking shape. A groundbreaking ceremony will be held this afternoon, and President Kong arrived from Nanjing last night to personally preside over the ceremony. The order of the ceremony and the wharf construction plan are detailed below:

Central Bank Investment and Construction

To develop international trade, support state-owned enterprises, and promote the prosperity of the Greater Shanghai area, the Central Bank decided to invest in the construction of the Qujiang Wharf and Warehouse in the spring of the 23rd year [of the Republic, i.e. 1934]. In September of that year, Chen Jì'ān, Ye Zhuótáng, Chá Délì, Liu Hongsheng, Song Ziliang, and others were appointed to organize the Qujiang Wharf Design Committee. In May of the 24th year [1935], Zhang Gongquan and Xu Keting were added as committee members to study all construction plans. By August, the design work was completed, and the Design Committee was reorganized into a Construction Committee, with the same members, and Song Ziliang was appointed as chairman to oversee the project. Construction has been underway for over a year, and various projects are taking shape. It has been decided that a groundbreaking ceremony will be held at 3:00 PM today.

Groundbreaking Ceremony Held Today

The groundbreaking ceremony for the wharf is scheduled to take place at 3:00 PM this afternoon, with the following order: 1. All stand at attention; 2. Play music; 3. Pay the highest respects to the Party, National Flag, and the Portrait of the Premier; 4. The Chairman respectfully reads the Premier's Will; 5. Chairman Kong delivers the opening remarks; 6. Song Ziliang, Chairman of the Qujiang Wharf Construction Committee, reports on the project plan and the progress of construction; 7. Minister Wu Dingchang, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, and others deliver speeches; 8. Perform the groundbreaking ceremony; 9. Refreshments; 10. Photography; Adjournment. The committee has distributed invitations, inviting people from all walks of life to participate in the ceremony. The route to and from the venue is as follows: from Yangshupu Road, turn into Dinghai Road, cross Dinghai Bridge, follow the west road of the Dinghai Island Dredging Bureau, to the north end of the Fish Market Ferry Terminal. The committee has arranged a special ferry to transport attendees.

Entire Plan Implemented in Three Phases

The Qujiang Wharf is located on the west bank of the Huangpu River, north of the Qujiang Estuary at No. 90 Shangzi. It encompasses over 800 mu of reclaimed land and over 300 mu of land within areas Zhou 1, 3, and 2. After purchasing and filling the land to 19.5 feet above the Wusong Datum, there will be over 3,000 feet of shoreline and over 1,000 feet of docks, all suitable for building wharves and warehouses. The entire plan is divided into three phases. The first phase will involve the construction of two wharves, two reinforced concrete warehouses, and two iron-roofed sheds, with a total construction cost of five million yuan. The location is in the southern section of the wharf area, accounting for one-third of the total area. Construction is underway and is expected to be completed by the end of this year, at which point operations can begin. If necessary, the second and third phases of the project will also be carried out. Upon completion of the entire plan, there will be 3,000 feet of straight-line wharf shoreline, eight four-story steel-framed warehouses, three iron-roofed sheds, and a barge port at the south end. The Puxi Road, a major arterial road in the city, will be located 1,000 feet behind the warehouses, running north and south. The Wuquan Road runs east and west, bisecting the area from the city center to the middle edge of the wharf. At the northern part of the wharf area, there is also a public wharf, 350 feet long. Within the wharf area, along both sides of Puxi Road, there is space reserved for the construction of travel agencies, shipping companies, transportation companies, automobile companies, hotels, and other agencies related to the wharf. As for the water supply equipment for ships, the fire protection of the wharf and warehouses, as well as security and sanitation issues, every effort is made to ensure convenience for passengers and those picking them up, with thorough and complete facilities. Separate routes are provided for passenger travel and cargo transportation, so as not to interfere with each other. There are reception rooms for passengers and those picking them up to rest, which also include shops selling food, beverages, and well-known Chinese products for passengers to purchase. Other facilities, such as observation decks, customs baggage and passport inspection offices, parking lots, police stations, and information centers, are also available. In short, passengers' stay, departure, and arrival are all made as convenient as possible.

Initial Phase to Be Completed by Year-End

The first phase of the project was originally scheduled for completion this autumn, but the arrival of the pilings ordered from the United States was delayed due to the US dockworkers' strike, so it will now be completed by the end of the year. The wharf was originally planned to be a single straight wharf, but a barge port, 220 feet long, is temporarily being built in the middle, causing the shoreline to curve inward, thus forming two wharves, each 590 feet long. The lower part is filled with wood pilings, and the upper part is constructed of reinforced concrete. The pilings are driven below the average waterline to prevent decay. The wharf deck is 50 feet wide and equipped with all berthing facilities. There are mooring pilings 50 feet apart and horizontal timbers for barges to moor. The deck has rotating cranes, and there is a lower deck to allow small boats and barges to operate normally when the tide is low. The above is the first phase of the project. After completion, each wharf can accommodate the largest liners entering and leaving the Huangpu River, and when the entire project is completed, the total length of the wharf will reach over 3,000 feet, allowing six large liners, each 500 feet long, to dock simultaneously.

Four Warehouse Buildings Constructed First

There are four warehouses standing behind the wharf. The two inside are reinforced concrete warehouses, which are permanent structures. The lower part is driven with 100-foot and 90-foot-long pilings, and the upper part is made of reinforced concrete. The foundation is designed for four stories, but the first phase will only construct two stories, with the remaining two stories to be added later when business expands. Each warehouse is 220 feet long and 130 feet wide, with the upper floor used for long-term storage and the lower floor for short-term storage. The two outside are iron-roofed sheds, which are temporary structures used for short-term storage. Each is 220 feet long and 80 feet wide, with three bridges connecting directly to the wharf deck. This is also part of the first phase of the project. When permanent steel-framed warehouses are rebuilt in the future, the iron-roofed sheds can be dismantled and moved to the rear for reuse.

Warehouse Capacity and Loading/Unloading Equipment

The current total volume of the warehouses is 15,000 tons. The wharf deck outside the warehouses is equipped with track-mounted cranes that can lift goods directly from the ship's hold to any floor of the steel-framed warehouses without the need for manual handling. In front of the warehouses, there is a duplex linear crane at the cargo inspection area that can lift goods directly from the lower level of the warehouses to the upper level. All cranes include four cargo transport vehicles, two inclined roller vehicles, and one one-ton and one six-ton mobile lifting vehicle. There are also 150 cargo roller trolleys. If necessary, several two-ton and ten-and-a-half-ton rotating cranes will be added. The rear of the warehouses is equipped with elevators, so the interior of the warehouses can maintain one-way traffic.

Offices and Staff Residences

The offices are located in the middle of the warehouses, along the barge port, and are two stories high, 220 feet long, and built of reinforced concrete and brick tiles. The upper floor is the wharf management office, and the lower floor is allocated as a customs inspection station and passenger reception room in accordance with the new customs regulations. At the southwest end of the wharf area, not far from the wharf warehouses, several staff residences have been built, including one residence for the wharf manager, two residences each for the wharf supervisors and customs inspectors, one staff dormitory that can accommodate 40 people, and six two-story houses with two rooms each, and twelve two-story houses with one room each.

Building Wuquan Road to Connect Various Areas

Within the wharf area, there are over 250,000 square feet of open space, divided into nine rectangular plots, reserved as bases for future warehouse construction. The perimeter is surrounded by roads paved with cinder to provide access to all directions. One of the wider roads leads directly to the northern gate, connecting with the Wuquan Road currently under construction. The road runs east-west, starting from the north end of the wharf, crossing the Jungong Road, and reaching the city center. It is being built jointly with the Shanghai Municipal Government, requiring a construction cost of 1.5 million yuan, and is scheduled to be completed at the same time as the first phase of the wharf construction. There are three traffic routes: 1. From Wuquan Road, turn into Jungong Road to reach Yangshupu Road; 2. From Wuquan Road, pass through the city center and turn into Qimei Road to reach Desway Road; 3. From Wuquan Road, pass through the city center and turn into Jiangwan Road to reach North Sichuan Road. The travel time by car on these three routes is less than 20 minutes, which is very convenient.

Discussion on Extending the Songhu Railway Line

In addition to highways, there are plans to extend the Songhu railway line to connect with the wharf. This railway will have one track located behind the warehouses, merging into one at the intersection of Wuquan Road, and connecting to the Songhu line along the Huangpu River north of the city center. The route is nine kilometers long, and according to estimates by the two railway bureaus, the construction cost will require 750,000 yuan and take about three months. The two parties are currently in discussions on joint construction. If construction can begin in the near future, it is hoped that it can be completed at the same time as the wharf. In the future, cargo loading and unloading can be directly handled by cranes, without the need to move goods to warehouses. Furthermore, there are several thousand acres of vacant land near the wharf. The Greater Shanghai plan originally included a plan to open an airport, and a designated area on the river surface for seaplane mooring. If this becomes a reality in the future, the transportation of goods at the wharf will not only have water and land connections, but will also achieve the combined transport effects of water, land, and air. This may be built when the entire plan is completed.

Business Conditions in the First Half of the Year 109

Major Banks All Have Profits National Goods Industry Also Shows Some Progress

According to inquiries with relevant parties, the business conditions of various industries in the city in the first half of the year are as follows: Major banks with strong capital reserves all have profits. Other banks are mostly able to maintain operations with difficulty. The exact situation will be clear around the 26th and 27th of this month, as they are currently busy closing accounts. The real estate industry appears to be slightly more active this period compared to the past, but there are still no large-scale transactions. In general, this industry has become a spent force due to the sluggish market. Although there are no accurate statistics on the industrial and commercial situation of the national goods industry last year, it is predicted that if the smuggling problem in North China can be stopped immediately, there will be better development in the second half of the year. Small industries have developed rapidly in recent years, but the profits are very small. This is mainly due to the shortage of capital, the lack of refinement in the output, and the weak sales. However, due to the very low expenses, they are all able to maintain operations without losses.

Various Qianzhuang Borrow Funds from the Three Banks to Be Repaid After the Summer Festival 110

The Three Banks Have Granted the Request

The Ministry of Finance previously allocated 25 million yuan in financial public bonds to rescue the qianzhuang industry, and established a qianzhuang industry supervision committee. The Bank of China, the Central Bank, and the Bank of Communications provided loans of 18 million yuan, while commercial banks and the qianzhuang reserve fund provided a total of 7 million yuan. Now, in addition to the 7 million yuan from commercial banks and the qianzhuang reserve fund, which has already been repaid, the 18 million yuan from the Bank of China, the Central Bank, and the Bank of Communications has been handled by the borrowing qianzhuang to repay the loans. As of yesterday's deadline, 14 million yuan had not yet been repaid. Now the borrowing qianzhuang have decided to wait until after the Summer Festival, when the funds received by industries and businesses will be transferred to the qianzhuang and then repaid. It is heard that the three banks have secured guarantees for these loans and have therefore granted the request.

British Ship Has Suspended Service to Lianyungang 111

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Cables Nanjing for Intervention The Ganzhou Cargo Ship Officially Discontinued Service to Laoyao Lianyungang, as an inland port of China, foreign ships are not usually allowed to call. The Taikoo Dockyard Company decided to suspend services of seven ships due to unprecedented recession of shipping routes along the coast, so as to reduce the losses of overcapacity. They then deployed the Ganzhou cargo ship to Laoyao for coal transportation and passenger and cargo loading, which sparked strong opposition from private shipping merchants in Shanghai.

They sent a cable to the central government requesting an injunction, fearing that if this precedent were allowed, not only British ships but also ships from other countries would compete. While the joint water-land transportation only allows Chinese-owned ships and private ships are not permitted, now it would be broken by the foreign merchants, such that in the future, all ports in inland China would be open to foreign ships, and how could national ships survive? At the same time, due to the direct conflict of interests, Cai Zengji of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company also sent an urgent cable to Nanjing

to Deputy Minister Yu Feipeng, requesting an effective injunction. Now it has been confirmed that Yu has discussed with the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Finance, and they have decided that foreign ships should be banned from sailing to the new inland port of Laoyao in accordance with the decision of the Executive Yuan. The combined cargo of the Longhai Railway will still be carried by Chinese-owned ships according to the original plan. The Longhai Railway Administration is requested to prevent foreign ships from berthing at the dock when they sail to Lianyungang as soon as possible. The local customs office is also notified to ban the customs clearance of foreign ships for export.

The above measures are the most effective way to maintain the right of navigation in inland ports and to prevent foreign forces from seizing the joint transportation of goods from the Northwest. The central government has already implemented this, and the Ganzhou cargo ship of the Taikoo Dockyard Company in Shanghai, which has been sailing to Lianyungang, has made three trips. It has now received this news and has automatically suspended its service, and has completely abandoned this route. At the same time, it has announced the official discontinuation of the Ganzhou cargo ship and will no longer sail it.

Shanghai, Zhejiang, and Wuxi Silk Industry Representatives Held a Joint Meeting Yesterday 113

Believe That the Grade Inspection Method Is Difficult to Implement Universally Elected Shanghai, Zhejiang, and Wuxi Representatives to Attend the Inspection Meeting Telegram to Zhejiang Unified Committee to Quickly Release the Detained Chunman Silk Factory The Shanghai Silk Industry Association held its fourth temporary representative meeting of the second session at the association's location on North Shansi Road at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, and also held a joint meeting with the Zhejiang and Wuxi silk industry representatives and associations to discuss the raw silk export grade inspection standards of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, and elected representatives to attend the meeting. The details are as follows:

Resolutions

Yesterday, representatives from the following silk factories attended: Xiexing, Jiuyu, Jiyu, Shifu, Qinyi, Yifeng, Hengtai, Xinglun, Yuanyu, Yuanji, Xinchang, Fuchang No. 1, Fuchang No. 2, Tailun, Hengcang, Hongtai, Heji, Changji, Liyuan, Dongxiang, Yufeng, Guangyuan, Tongyu, Dafeng, Shaoxing, Dacheng, Baotai, Gansheng, Yutai, Qiaoyuan, Xingchang, Yihe, etc. Silk factory representatives Shen Huachen, Wang Xiaoxiang, Zhang Peishen, Huang Jiwen, etc., Zhejiang silk industry representatives Jiang Laixian, Zhu Jingan, Wuxi silk industry representatives Qian Fenghao, Wang Huanan, Xu Shouyi, Zheng Haiquan, Cheng Bingruo, Wang Xieming, Cao Shaochen, and others, a total of 50 people, were present. After Chairman Shen Huachen reported on the purpose of the meeting, he read the draft of the raw silk export grade inspection standards set by the Commodity Inspection Bureau, the original letter calling for the meeting, and the instructions from the Shanghai Municipal Party Committee and Social Affairs Bureau regarding the registration of silk factory workers. Then, the discussion began: The draft of the raw silk export grade inspection standards set by the Commodity Inspection Bureau was discussed and resolved that this standard adopts the Japanese silk inspection method used in the Japanese market. In China, due to the differences in silk factory machinery, the types of silk have not been unified, and the skills of workers have not been properly trained, so it cannot be universally implemented. Regarding the Commodity Inspection Bureau's call for a meeting of silk manufacturers at 2:00 PM on June 22nd to discuss the raw silk export grade inspection, it was resolved that Shanghai would send Shen Huachen and Huang Jiwen as representatives, Wuxi would send Qian Fenghao and Cheng Bingruo, and Zhejiang would send Chu Jisen and Zhu Jingan. Regarding the detention of Chunman silk factories by the Zhejiang Provincial Silk Control Committee for receiving addresses that are below standard, it was resolved to telegram Zhejiang Province again to quickly release the detained Chunman silk factory. Regarding the order from the Shanghai Municipal Party Committee and Social Affairs Bureau to conduct the registration of Shanghai silk factory workers, it was resolved to send a letter to the silk industry trade unions in each district to explain the meaning of registration to the workers before proceeding with the registration. The meeting adjourned around 7:00 PM.

Inspection Procedures

The Commodity Inspection Bureau stipulates the raw silk grade inspection guidelines and procedures: 1. Batching: Each batch should have five pieces of the same raw silk and should not have different numbers. 2. White cloth bags: The white cloth bags for packaging raw silk must be 4.04 city feet long, 3.12 city feet wide, and 3.6 city feet high, and must be prepared by each silk factory. (These cloth bags are used for packing exports, and the material must be strong.) Attachment: Diagram (omitted). 3. Canvas bags: These canvas bags must be made by each factory according to the following specifications. (Diagram omitted) 4. Silk quantity: The quantity of silk in each piece must not exceed or be less than 5% of 60.33 kg (or 133 pounds). (For those calculated in old jin, it must not exceed 105 jin or be less than 95 jin.) Each piece should contain 15 small bundles for the old style and 28 small bundles for the new style. 5. Delivery: The silk factory delivers the goods to the exporter according to the contract. All raw silk should be sent to the Commodity Inspection Bureau, Silk Group Warehouse (3rd floor) at 1040 North Suzhou Road, Shanghai, and a request form must be attached, stating the type and number of silk, and the number of each piece, as well as the names of the requester and exporter. This request form should be prepared by the requester, and the style can be obtained from the Commodity Inspection Bureau. When requesting, the public measurement inspection fee must be paid according to regulations. If it is spot goods, the above procedures should be followed, but the name of the export commodity should not be filled in. 6. Visual inspection: After receiving the raw silk, a visual inspection will be conducted. The exporter or buyer may watch during the inspection. The visual inspection focuses on one end of each bundle and pays attention to the following points (by touching). The results must be recorded in detail. 7. Sampling: After the visual inspection is completed, samples are taken for grade inspection. 25 strands are randomly selected from each batch for grade inspection, and about 16 strands are selected for public measurement inspection. After sampling, a lead seal is placed on the bag. After the inspection is completed, the samples are sealed and returned to the requester. However, the samples for grade inspection can be sent to the location designated by the requester. 8. Mechanical inspection: 1. Cutting inspection (speed according to US regulations); 2. Strand inspection: A. Average strand; (calculated in public measurement) B. Strand deviation; C. Strand difference; (e.g., A grade 13/15, must not be coarser than 14.55 or finer than 13.45); 3. Tensile inspection: A. Tensile strength (centimeters) B. Elongation (percentage); 4. Cohesion inspection: Dupont method; 5. Uniformity inspection: Uniform average score and minimum average score; 6. Cleanness inspection; 7. Neatness inspection. 9. Certificates: The grade certificate specifies the quantity of the batch, the results of each inspection, and the grade of the batch. The public measurement certificate is issued as usual. 10. Grades: The grade list for yellow and white raw silk is as follows (Table omitted) Grading instructions: 1. The comprehensive percentage of the main inspection is calculated from the results obtained from the four inspections of average uniformity, minimum uniformity, cleanness, and neatness. The calculation method is "average uniformity" multiplied by 30, "minimum uniformity" multiplied by 30, "cleanness" multiplied by 20, "neatness" multiplied by 20, and the results of each item are added together to obtain the comprehensive percentage. 2. Grade evaluation: Each batch of raw silk should use (A) the comprehensive percentage of a certain grade, (B) the minimum score prescribed for each item in the main and auxiliary inspections, and 3. the result of the visual inspection. If there is uneven color or inconsistent silk texture, the grade of the batch of raw silk should be reduced by one grade compared to the grade obtained by grading.

following requirements, by each factory monthly. (Diagram omitted) 4. Silk Amount: Silk amount for each piece must not exceed or be less than 5% of 60.33 Kilogrammes (or 133 pounds). (For calculating in old Jin, do not exceed 105 Jin, or less than 95 Jin.) For each old type package it should be packaged into fifteen small bundles, for new type twenty-eight small bundles. 5. Exchange of Goods: Silk factories exchange goods according to contracts with the exporter, where all raw silk should be sent to Shanghai North Suzhou Road number 1040 Commodity Inspection Bureau, Silk Group Warehouse, (3rd level) along with the attach request form, indicate with the type of silk amount, the number of each piece, the applicant and the exporter’s names, etc. This request form should be placed by the applicant, to be claimed from the Commodity Inspection Bureau, and according to related regulations, the public amount inspection fee should be attached when applying. If they are currently goods, they should follow the existing procedures, just without filling out the exported goods name. 6. Naked Eye Inspection: After the raw silk is received, they will hold a naked eye inspection. The exporter or the buyer may watch the inspection, the naked eye inspection for each bag must pay attention to the following points (using hand to touch) after examination, it is necessary to record in detail, 7. Take Samples: After the naked eye inspection is completed, samples will be taken for grading inspection, each batch will take about twenty five strips, Public quantity inspection roughly takes sixteen strip, after taking a sample, they place a lead seal, after inspection is complete, they seal up the sample strip, and return it to the applicant, however, with the sample strips for grading inspection, they can send the sample to the place which the applicant appointed to. 8. Tension (cm) 乙. Elongation, (percentage) Four, cohesion inspection, Dupont method. Five Uniformity inspection, uniformity average score and lowest average score Six Cleanness inspection. Seven Neatness inspection. 9. Certificate: The product certificate, stating one batch of the quantity and each inspection result and which the grade of that batch, the public amount certification, which is issued according to regulations. 10. City Police Bureau: Large Parade of Senior Police Yesterday 114

At the Naval Training Ground on Longhua Road

Since taking office, the director of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, Mr. Cai Jinjun, has spared no effort in reforming the city's police administration. He has been particularly active in training senior police officers. In addition to the police trainees trained by the Police Training School, he has also transferred and concentrated active senior police officers from various branch bureaus and teams for rigorous training. Two training sessions have already been completed with excellent results, and training is still ongoing. Yesterday marked the completion of the third session of the concentrated training team. A general review was held at the naval training ground on Longhua Road in the city. Graduating police trainees from the training school and the police chief class were also ordered to participate in the review. More than a thousand senior police officers attended. Wang Xiong, the chief of the police force, served as the general commander. All branch bureau chiefs and bureau-level directors and above also attended. The mayor was invited to personally review the troops, and the ceremony was quite grand. At 5:00 AM yesterday, training teams from various locations arrived one after another for preliminary drills. By 7:30 AM, all officials and police officers were present. At 8:00 AM, the mayor and Director Cai entered the field, accompanied by General Commander Wang Xiong, Chief Inspector Wang Dasui, Deputy Chief Inspector Tong Guangfu, Director of the Training Section Xu Taikong, and others for a week-long inspection of the troops. This was followed by a marching parade, led by the bureau's military band. Fortunately, the weather yesterday was cloudy and rain-free, with a suitable climate. All police officers were in high spirits, with serious attitudes and orderly paces, displaying great vigor. After the marching parade, Director Cai recited the Party members' code of conduct and the military discipline instructions. The entire assembly stood at attention and listened respectfully. The mayor then gave a speech, stating, "The relationship between the police and self-governance is extremely close. Self-governance requires accurate household registration, which is essential before any undertaking can commence. This task rests on the shoulders of the police. The central government has scheduled the convocation of the National Assembly in November of this year to promulgate the constitution, which will serve as the foundation for constitutional government. Therefore, the police bear the greatest responsibility for local self-governance," and so on. Director Cai then gave a speech, stating, "The main points of the mayor's instructions are that the bureau's past efforts in investigating household registration, promoting literacy education, carrying out the Baojia system, and rigorously conducting training have all been guided by these principles, aiming to achieve the goals of police-public integration and public-police integration," and so on.

Simple and Beautiful Savings Box Design

Starting with School Children

The bureau's new safety deposit boxes total more than 3,000, in various sizes, with the latest types of safety doors and other features, similar to those of the Four Banks Savings Association.
